<p class="gb-text gb-text-7ae02d38">Sarah – Home Cook &amp; Recipe Creator</p>



<p class="gb-text gb-text-455e644f">I’m Sarah, a 37-year-old mom with a deep love for cooking and a passion for making mealtime simple, tasty, and stress-free. I know how busy life can get, which is why I created Yum Yum Recipes — a space to share my favorite easy-to-make meals, practical kitchen tips, and time-saving tricks to help you enjoy cooking every day.</p>
